# **long_tail_account_transfer_result_query**
> LongTailResponse long_tail_account_transfer_result_query(long_tail_request=long_tail_request)

Long-tail wrapper for `Common_AccountTransferResultQuery`

Forwards the `Common_AccountTransferResultQuery` GraphQL operation to Monarch and returns the
raw `data` payload inside the shared `LongTailResponse` envelope.
Variables (if any) are passed under `variables` in the request body.
Shape is opaque; do not pin clients to deep field paths.
